# Eastward Expansion (Danzig Ceded)
country_event = {
	id = poland.1
	title = poland.1.t
	desc = poland.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.1.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_ideas = fascist_influence
		add_state_claim = 198
		add_state_claim = 199
		add_state_claim = 201
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.1.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = medium_increase }
	}
}

# Soviet Union Demands the East
country_event = {
	id = poland.2
	title = poland.2.t
	desc = poland.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_tanks_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.2.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 30 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					any_other_country = {
						is_major = yes
						OR = {
							is_in_faction_with = POL
							has_guaranteed = POL
						}
					}
					has_idea = anti_soviet_pact
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			SOV = {
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 96 controls_state = 96 } }
					transfer_state = 96
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 95 controls_state = 95 } }
					transfer_state = 95
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 933 controls_state = 933 } }
					transfer_state = 933
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 94 controls_state = 94 } }
					transfer_state = 94
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 93 controls_state = 93 } }
					transfer_state = 93
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 91 controls_state = 91 } }
					transfer_state = 91
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 89 controls_state = 89 } }
					transfer_state = 89
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 97 controls_state = 97 } }
					transfer_state = 97
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 784 controls_state = 784 } }
					transfer_state = 784
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 996 controls_state = 996 } }
					transfer_state = 996
				}
				if = {
					limit = { POL = { owns_state = 997 controls_state = 977 } }
					transfer_state = 997
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = {country_event = { id = poland.3} }
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.2.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			SOV = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = POL
					generator = { 96 95 933 94 93 91 89 97 784 996 997 }
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = poland.4 } }
	}
}

# Poland Cedes the East
country_event = {
	id = poland.3
	title = poland.3.t
	desc = poland.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_tanks_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.3.a
		if = {
			limit = { 
				POL = { 
					owns_state = 96
					controls_state = 96 
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 96
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				POL = { 
					owns_state = 95
					controls_state = 95 
				}
			}
			transfer_state = 95
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				POL = { 
					owns_state = 933
					controls_state = 933

			add_state_claim = 5

		}

# Poland Granted Eastern Germany
country_event = {
	id = poland.8
	title = poland.8.t
	desc = poland.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_tanks_01
	
	trigger = {
		POL = { has_country_flag = POL_accepted_soviet_protection }
		tag = POL
		SOV = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 5
				owns_state = 63
				owns_state = 1112
				owns_state = 68
				owns_state = 66
				owns_state = 67
				owns_state = 797
				owns_state = 801
				owns_state = 802
				owns_state = 803
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = POL_accepted_soviet_protection
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.8.a
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 5 } }
			transfer_state = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 63 } }
			transfer_state = 63
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 1112 } }
			transfer_state = 1112
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 68 } }
			transfer_state = 68
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 66 } }
			transfer_state = 66
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 67 } }
			transfer_state = 67
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 797 } }
			transfer_state = 797
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 801 } }
			transfer_state = 801
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 802 } }
			transfer_state = 802
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SOV = { owns_state = 803 } }
			transfer_state = 803
		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = poland.9 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = poland.12
	title = poland.12.t
	desc = poland.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_tanks_01
	
	trigger = {
		tag = POL
		has_completed_focus = POL_artillery_modernisation
		has_government = neutrality
		has_war_with = ITA
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
		417 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = POL
					is_in_faction_with = POL			
				}
				has_war_with = ITA
			}
		}
		OR = {
			divisions_in_state = {
				state = 162
				size > 0
			}
			divisions_in_state = {
				state = 157
				size > 0
			}
			divisions_in_state = {
				state = 2
				size > 0
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = poland.12.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = WOJTEK_COMMANDER
		hidden_effect = {
			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Wojtek"
				portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/POL/Portrait_POL_Voytek.dds"
				traits = { bearer_of_artillery }
				skill = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = POL_vojtek_commander
		}
	}

}
	
# Invitation to Polish Intermarium Faction
country_event = {
	id = poland.13
	title = poland.13.t
	desc = poland.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_summit
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.13.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.15
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = POL
					ratio > 0.85
				}
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = POL
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				ROOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = poland.14
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { has_government = neutrality }
				ROOT = { has_government = neutrality }
			}
			add_ideas = POL_Sanacja_Influence
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "POL"
			value = 300
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.13.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }
		POL = { country_event = poland.15 }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.16.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				POL = { has_completed_focus = POL_Reaffirm_Ties_With_Romania }
			}
			modifier = {
				HUN = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = POL
					ratio > 0.85
				}
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						is_in_faction_with = POL
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.02
				ROOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = poland.18
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { has_government = neutrality }

			}

		}

			type = alliance
			id = "POL"
			value = 300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
				modifier = {
					HUN = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL } }
					factor = 0.05
				}
			}
		POL = { country_event = poland.19 }
	}
}

						is_in_faction_with = POL
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				ROOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
			}
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = poland.18
			add_to_faction = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = { has_government = neutrality }
				ROOT = { has_government = neutrality }
			}
			add_ideas = POL_Sanacja_Influence
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "POL"
			value = 300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
				modifier = {
					ROM = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL } }
					factor = 0.1
				}
			}
		POL = { country_event = poland.19 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = poland.30
	title = poland.30.t
	desc = poland.30.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_meeting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.30.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = POL
					ratio > 0.15
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				GER = { 
					owns_state = 188
					controls_state = 188 
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				GER = { 
					owns_state = 85
					controls_state = 85 
				}
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.31 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.30.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 85
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = alliance
			id = "GER"
			value = 200
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = befriend
			id = "GER"
			value = 200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER = { is_subject = no }
				GER = { has_civil_war = no }
				POL = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
				63 = { is_controlled_by = GER }
			}
			GER = { country_event = poland.195 }
			else = { GER = { set_country_flag = POL_GER_Pressure_Danzig_Response } }
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.32 }
	}
}

	desc = poland.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_danzig_boat
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.33.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = POL value > 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = GER value < 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = POL value > 15 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				has_opinion = { target = GER value < -15 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			}
		}
		POL = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = POL_League_Support } }
		GER = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = POL_League_Opposition } }
		POL = { country_event = poland.34 }
		ROOT = { set_country_flag = POL_Voted_Yes }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.33.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
					has_opinion = { target = POL value < 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
					has_opinion = { target = GER value > 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
					has_opinion = { target = POL value < -15 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
					has_opinion = { target = GER value > 15 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ROOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
			}
		}
		POL = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = POL_League_Opposition } }
		GER = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = POL_League_Support } }
		POL = { country_event = poland.35 }
		ROOT = { set_country_flag = POL_Voted_No }
	}
}

#Beck-Ribbentrop - German decision
country_event = {
	id = poland.77
	title = poland.77.t
	desc = poland.77.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_josef_beck
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.77.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = { diplomatic_relation = { country = SOV relation = non_aggression_pact active = no } }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = POL
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			}
			GER = {
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { has_government = neutrality } }
			POL = { set_country_flag = POL_was_neutral }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { has_government = democratic } }
			POL = { set_country_flag = POL_was_democracy }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { has_government = fascism } }
			POL = { set_country_flag = POL_was_fascist }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { has_government = communism } }
			POL = { set_country_flag = POL_was_communist }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				AND = { 
					has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor"
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Ribbentrop_Beck_tooltip_DOD
			hidden_effect = {
				GER = { 
					set_autonomy = {
						target = POL
						autonomous_state = autonomy_satellite
						freedom_level = 0.80
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory"}
					custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Ribbentrop_Beck_tooltip_TFV
					hidden_effect = {
						GER = { 
							set_autonomy = {
								target = POL
								autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
								freedom_level = 0.80
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Ribbentrop_Beck_tooltip
						hidden_effect = {
							GER = { puppet = POL }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			DNZ = { country_event = poland.58 }
			POL = { add_ideas = POL_Ribbentrop_Beck_Pact }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_government = neutrality } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality #game will crash if this part isn't included
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_government = fascism } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascism #game will crash if this part isn't included
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_government = democratic } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic #game will crash if this part isn't included
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { GER = { has_government = communism } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism #game will crash if this part isn't included
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_was_neutral } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.6
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_was_communist } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = communism
						popularity = 0.6
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_was_democracy } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.6
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_was_fascist } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = fascism
						popularity = 0.6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.78 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.77.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.79 }
	}
}

#Romanian Intervention - Ban Communism
country_event = {
	id = poland.92
	title = poland.92.t
	desc = poland.92.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_josef_beck
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.92.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = POL
					ratio < 0.4
				}
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.93 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.92.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					ROM = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
					ROM = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					ROM = { is_in_faction_with = FRA }
					ROM = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
					ROM = { is_in_faction_with = ITA }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.4
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = POL
					ratio > 0.65
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = POL
					ratio > 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				AND = {
					has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor"
					POL = { has_government = fascism }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Romanian_Intervention_tooltip_DOD
			hidden_effect = {
				POL = { 
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ROM
						autonomous_state = autonomy_satellite
						freedom_level = 0.55
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory"}
					custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Romanian_Intervention_tooltip_TFV
					hidden_effect = {
						POL = { 
							set_autonomy = {
								target = ROM
								autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
								freedom_level = 0.55
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Romanian_Intervention_tooltip
						hidden_effect = {
							POL = { puppet = ROM }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.15
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.94 }
	}
}

#Poland Wants to join Japanese Faction
country_event = {
	id = poland.97
	title = poland.97.t
	desc = poland.97.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_Jan_Kowalewski
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.97.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					exists = yes
					#NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
					#is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			add_ideas = POL_Polish_Military_Mission
			ROOT = {
				add_to_faction = POL
			}
			if = {
				limit = { POL = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = SOV } }
				POL = { diplomatic_relation = { country = SOV relation = non_aggression_pact active = no } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					POL = { NOT = { has_war_with = SOV } }
					JAP = { has_war_with = SOV }
				}
				POL = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = SOV
						type = take_state_focus
						generator = { 206 } 
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { news_event = poland.100 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.97.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SOV = { surrender_progress > 0.55 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SOV = { surrender_progress > 0.8 }
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.101 }
	}
}

#Poland invites Japan
country_event = {
	id = poland.99
	title = poland.99.t
	desc = poland.99.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_Jan_Kowalewski
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.99.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					exists = yes
					#NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
					#is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			add_ideas = POL_Polish_Military_Mission
			POL = {
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { POL = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = SOV } }
				POL = { diplomatic_relation = { country = SOV relation = non_aggression_pact active = no } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					POL = { NOT = { has_war_with = SOV } }
					JAP = { has_war_with = SOV }
				}
				POL = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = SOV
						type = take_state_focus
						generator = { 206 } 
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = { news_event = poland.100 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.99.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SOV = { surrender_progress > 0.55 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SOV = { surrender_progress > 0.8 }
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.101 }
	}
}

#Czechoslovakian Response
country_event = {
	id = poland.105
	title = poland.105.t
	desc = poland.105.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_josef_beck
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Yield to Polish Demands
		name = poland.105.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = { # Decrease chance ROM guarantees CZE
				ROM = { 
					has_guaranteed = CZE
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
				}
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = { # If they stand a chance they will fight
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = POL
					ratio > 0.75
				}
				NOT = {
					any_neighbor_country = {
						NOT = { tag = POL }
						is_in_faction_with = POL
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #if you lead a faction, fight
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05 #if you are in a faction, maybe fight
				is_faction_leader = no
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_puppet = yes
				NOT = { is_puppet_of = POL } #puppeted CZE wouldn't surrender Sudetenland otherwise
			}
			modifier = { # Increase it again if other bordering nations are in Polish Faction
				any_neighbor_country = {
					NOT = { tag = POL }
					is_in_faction_with = POL
				}
				factor = 2.0
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.106 }
	}
	
	option = { # Refuse anyway
		name = poland.105.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 10 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = POL
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		POL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = POL_demands_rejected }
			country_event = poland.107
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = CZE
					generator = { 70 71 72 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Czechoslovakia Yields
country_event = {
	id = poland.106
	title = poland.106.t
	desc = poland.106.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_occupy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.106.a
		if = {
			limit = { 70 = { is_owned_by = CZE } }
			POL = { transfer_state = 70 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 71 = { is_owned_by = CZE } }
			POL = { transfer_state = 71 }
			71 = {	add_core_of = POL }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 72 = { is_owned_by = CZE } }
			POL = { transfer_state = 72 }
			72 = {	add_core_of = POL }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				HUN = { exists = yes }
				OR = { 
					if = {
						73 = { is_owned_by = CZE }
						664 = { is_owned_by = CZE }
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = { country_event = poland.108 }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { 664 = { is_owned_by = CZE } }
					POL = { transfer_state = 664 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 73 = { is_owned_by = CZE } }
					POL = { transfer_state = 73 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Dmowski's Death
news_event = {
	id = poland.113
	title = poland.113.t
	desc = poland.113.d
	picture = GFX_Dmowski_Funeral
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = POL
		country_exists = POL
		date > 1939.1.1
		NOT = { has_global_flag = Dmowski_dead }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 22
    }   
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_completed_focus = POL_The_Endecja_Movement }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Tadeusz Bielecki"
					desc = "POLITICS_Tadeusz_Bielecki_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_Tadeusz_Bielecki.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = conservatism
					traits = {
						polish_nationalist
						political_pragmatist
						dislikes_germany
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = Dmowski_dead
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.113.e
	}
	
}

#Molotov-Beck - Soviet decision
country_event = {
	id = poland.115
	title = poland.115.t
	desc = poland.115.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_josef_beck
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.115.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = POL
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
			}
			SOV = {
				declare_war_on = {
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { has_government = neutrality } }
			POL = { set_country_flag = POL_was_neutral2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { has_government = democratic } }
			POL = { set_country_flag = POL_was_democracy2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { has_government = fascism } }
			POL = { set_country_flag = POL_was_fascist2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { POL = { has_government = communism } }
			POL = { set_country_flag = POL_was_communist2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				AND = { 
					has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor"
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Beck_Molotov_tooltip_DOD
			hidden_effect = {
				SOV = { 
					set_autonomy = {
						target = POL
						autonomous_state = autonomy_satellite
						freedom_level = 0.55
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_dlc = "Together for Victory"}
					custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Beck_Molotov_tooltip_TFV
					hidden_effect = {
						SOV = { 
							set_autonomy = {
								target = POL
								autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
								freedom_level = 0.55
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						custom_effect_tooltip = POL_Beck_Molotov_tooltip
						hidden_effect = {
							SOV = { puppet = POL }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			DNZ = { country_event = poland.58 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { SOV = { has_government = neutrality } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality #game will crash if this part isn't included
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { SOV = { has_government = fascism } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascism #game will crash if this part isn't included
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { SOV = { has_government = democratic } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic #game will crash if this part isn't included
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { SOV = { has_government = communism } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism #game will crash if this part isn't included
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_was_neutral2 } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = neutrality
						popularity = 0.6
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_was_communist2 } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = communism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = communism
						popularity = 0.6
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_was_democracy2 } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.6
					}
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = { POL = { has_country_flag = POL_was_fascist2 } }
				POL = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = fascism
						popularity = 0.6
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Tymczasowy Rząd Jedności Narodowej"
					desc = "PROVISIONAL_GOVERNMENT_OF_NATIONAL_UNITY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_Provisional_Government_of_National_Unity.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = stalinism
					traits = {
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { POL = { has_completed_focus = POL_Seek_Autonomy } }
					NOT = { POL = { has_completed_focus = POL_Draw_Closer_To_The_USSR } }
				}
				POL = { set_party_name = { ideology = communism long_name = POL_ZPP_party_long name = POL_ZPP_party } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { POL = { has_completed_focus = POL_The_Polish_Socialist_Party } }
					NOT = { POL = { has_completed_focus = POL_The_Endecja_Movement } }
				}
				POL = { set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = POL_PSL_long name = POL_PSL_party } }
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.116 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.115.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.117 }
	}
}

		name = poland.124.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				67 = { 
					owner = {
						POL = {
							strength_ratio = {
								tag = PREV
								ratio < 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = take_state_focus
			generator = { 67 } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CZE = { is_in_faction_with = POL } }
			CZE = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = antagonize
					id = "GER"			
					value = 50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.124.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				67 = { 
					owner = {
						has_civil_war = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_political_power = -100
	}
}

			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
					has_government = neutrality
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					SOV = { has_guaranteed = LIT }
					LIT = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
					LIT = { is_puppet_of = SOV }
					NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					GER = { has_guaranteed = LIT }
					LIT = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					LIT = { is_puppet_of = GER }
					NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					ENG = { has_guaranteed = LIT }
					LIT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
					LIT = { is_puppet_of = ENG }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					FRA = { has_guaranteed = LIT }
					LIT = { is_in_faction_with = FRA }
					LIT = { is_puppet_of = FRA }
					NOT = { has_war_with = FRA }
				}
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = take_state_focus
			target = LIT
			generator = { 11 189 879 }
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 1 name = POL_Lithuanian_Constitutional_Crisis }
	}
}

#Minsk or War Response
country_event = {
	id = poland.138
	title = poland.138.t
	desc = poland.138.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_minsk_aerial_view
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.138.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = POL
						ratio > 0.7
					}
					surrender_progress < 0.2
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 206 = { owner = { owns_state = 207 controls_state = 207 } } }
			POL = { transfer_state = 207 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 206 = { owner = { owns_state = 204 controls_state = 204 } } }
			POL = { transfer_state = 204 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 206 = { owner = { owns_state = 194 controls_state = 194 } } }
			POL = { transfer_state = 194 }
		}
		POL = { transfer_state = 206 }
		POL = { country_event = poland.139 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.138.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				OR = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = POL
						ratio < 0.6
					}
					surrender_progress > 0.2
				}
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.140 }
	}
}

#German Intervention if Poland breaks away
country_event = {
	id = poland.149
	title = poland.149.t
	desc = poland.149.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_partisans2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.149.a
		declare_war_on = { target = POL type = annex_everything }
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				surrender_progress > 0.7
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.149.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				surrender_progress < 0.6
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Czech Arms Deal With Poland
country_event = {
	id = poland.150
	title = poland.150.t
	desc = poland.150.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_pzl24
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.150.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = HUN
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				tag = CZE 
			}
			add_political_power = 25
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = POL_CZE_Arms_Deal
				days = 500
			}
			army_experience = 10
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = POL_New_Line
		POL = {
			country_event = poland.151
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = POL_Arms_Deal_Dummy
					days = 500
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = POL_Arms_Deal
					days = 500
				}
			}
			air_experience = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.150.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_in_faction_with = POL
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.152 }
		hidden_effect = {
			POL = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = POL_Arms_Imports
					days = 500
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = poland.154.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_mansion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.154.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				546 = { is_controlled_by = ENG }
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					tag = ENG 
				}
				add_political_power = 200
			}
			POL = {
				country_event = poland.155
				add_political_power = -200
				transfer_state = 546
				hidden_effect = {
					546 = { 
						add_resource = {
							type = chromium
							amount = 5
							state = 546
						}
						add_resource = {
							type = tungsten
							amount = 7
							state = 546
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.154.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 35
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.153 }
	}
}

							type = chromium
							amount = 5
							state = 546
						}
						add_resource = {
							type = tungsten
							amount = 7
							state = 546
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

#Liberia decision
country_event = {
	id = poland.156
	title = poland.156.t
	desc = poland.156.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_mansion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.156.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
			}
			POL = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = LIB
					autonomous_state = autonomy_colony
					freedom_level = 0.8
				}
			}
			else = {
				POL = { puppet = LIB }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				298 = { is_controlled_by = LIB is_owned_by = LIB }
			}
			298 = {
				add_resource = {
					type = rubber
					amount = 5
					state = 298
				}
			}
		}
		LIB = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 298 }
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = POL_Offer_Liberia_Protection_1
			}
			add_ideas = free_trade
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.157 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.156.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 20
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.153 }
	}
}

		tag = POL

		has_war = no
		NOT = { GER = { is_justifying_wargoal_against = POL } }
		NOT = { SOV = { is_justifying_wargoal_against = POL } }
		NOT = { GER = { has_wargoal_against = POL } }
		NOT = { SOV = { has_wargoal_against = POL } }

		OR = {
			has_idea = extensive_conscription
			has_idea = service_by_requirement
			has_idea = all_adults_serve
			has_idea = scraping_the_barrel
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 25
    }

		name = poland.162.a
		add_ideas = limited_conscription
		add_stability = 0.025
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.162.b
		add_ideas = volunteer_only
		add_stability = 0.075
	}
}

				factor = 0
				POL = { has_war_with = FRA }
				NOT = { SOV = { has_war_with = FRA } }
			}

				factor = 0

				NOT = { SOV = { has_war_with = ENG } }

	}

			limit = { is_historical_focus_on = yes }

		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_historical_focus_on = no }
			POL = { random_list = {
					55 = {

					}
					45 = {
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.176.a
	}
}

#Border Conflict with Danzig, Pick Combatant
country_event = {
	id = poland.194
	title = poland.194.t
	desc = poland.194.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_danzig_police
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Danzig Fights
	option = {
		name = poland.194.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = GER
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		DNZ = {
			set_country_flag = Gdansk_POL_Border_War_For_Danzig
		}
		start_border_war = {
			change_state_after_war = no
			attacker = {
				state = 85
				num_provinces = 2
				on_win = Gdansk_poland_border_conflict.2
				on_lose = Gdansk_poland_border_conflict.3
				on_cancel = Gdansk_poland_border_conflict.4
			}
			
			defender = {
				state = 713
				num_provinces = 1
				on_win = Gdansk_poland_border_conflict.3
				on_lose = Gdansk_poland_border_conflict.2
				on_cancel = Gdansk_poland_border_conflict.4
			}
		}
		random_country =  {
			limit = { 
				original_tag = DNZ
				has_country_flag = Gdansk_POL_Border_War_For_Danzig
			}
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = POL decision = Gdansk_POL_border_conflict_time_until_cancelled }
		}
		random_country =  {
			limit = { 
				original_tag = DNZ
				has_country_flag = Gdansk_POL_Border_War_For_Danzig
			}
			POL = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = Gdansk_POL_border_conflict_time_until_cancelled }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Germany Fights
	option = {
		name = poland.194.b
		trigger = {
			GER = {
				has_country_flag = POL_GER_Danzig_Interverntion
				is_subject = no
				has_civil_war = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = POL }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = POL }
			}
			63 = { is_controlled_by = GER }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		GER = {
			set_country_flag = Danzig_POL_Border_War_For_Danzig
		}
		start_border_war = {
			change_state_after_war = no
			attacker = {
				state = 85
				num_provinces = 4
				on_win = Danzig_poland_border_conflict.2
				on_lose = Danzig_poland_border_conflict.3
				on_cancel = Danzig_poland_border_conflict.4
			}
			
			defender = {
				state = 63
				num_provinces = 4
				on_win = Danzig_poland_border_conflict.3
				on_lose = Danzig_poland_border_conflict.2
				on_cancel = Danzig_poland_border_conflict.4
			}
		}
		random_country =  {
			limit = { 
				original_tag = GER
				has_country_flag = Danzig_POL_Border_War_For_Danzig
			}
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = POL decision = Danzig_POL_border_conflict_escalate_to_war }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = POL decision = Danzig_POL_border_conflict_time_until_cancelled }
		}
		random_country =  {
			limit = {
				original_tag = GER
				has_country_flag = Danzig_POL_Border_War_For_Danzig
			}
			POL = {
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = Danzig_POL_border_conflict_escalate_conflict }
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = GER decision = Danzig_POL_border_conflict_time_until_cancelled }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Will Germany back Danzig?

	desc = poland.195.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#Germany is willing to back Danzig militarily

				factor = 0

			}

		set_country_flag = POL_GER_Pressure_Danzig_Response
		custom_effect_tooltip = POL_GER_Yes_Danzig_Intervention
	}
	
	#Germany is unwilling to back Danzig militarily
	option = {
		name = poland.195.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		clr_country_flag = POL_GER_Danzig_Interverntion
		set_country_flag = POL_GER_Pressure_Danzig_Response
		custom_effect_tooltip = POL_GER_No_Danzig_Intervention
	}

#Three way choice for Capitulation (Sanacja only)
country_event = {
	id = poland.196
	title = poland.196.t
	desc = poland.196.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_exile_meeting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		#Sikorski
		name = poland.196.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_war_with = ENG
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FRA }
					}
					AND = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Władysław Sikorski"
			desc = "POLITICS_WLADYSLAW_SIKORSKI_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Poland_Wladyslaw_Sikorski.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = liberalism
			traits = {
				democratic_reformer
			}
		}
	}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_completed_focus = SOV_claims_on_poland
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_idea = SOV_molotov_ribbentrop_pact
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = POL } }
			SOV = { add_political_power = 10 }
			add_named_threat = { threat = -1 name = POL_Renew_The_Polish_Soviet_Nonaggression_Pact }
			POL = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = SOV
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
				add_political_power = 10
				country_event = poland.203
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = poland.202.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.204 }
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = poland.208.t
	desc = poland.208.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_maczek_netherlands
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = POL
		POL = { has_capitulated = yes }
		POL = { is_puppet = no }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
    }
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = POL_exile_generals
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { has_unit_leader = 3160 } }
			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Stanisław Maczek"
				picture = "Stanislaw_Maczek.dds"
				traits = { armor_officer panzer_leader hill_fighter trait_mountaineer }
				id = 3160
				skill = 5
				attack_skill = 5
				defense_skill = 4
				planning_skill = 3
				logistics_skill = 4
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { has_unit_leader = 3176 } }
			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Bronisław Prugar-Ketling"
				picture = "Bronislaw_Prugar_Ketling.dds"
				traits = { ranger camouflage_expert }
				id = 3176
				skill = 3
				attack_skill = 3
				defense_skill = 4

				logistics_skill = 2
			}
		}
		if = {

			create_corps_commander = {
				name = "Stanisław Kopański"
				picture = "Portrait_POL_Stanislaw_Kopamski.dds"

				name = "Bolesław Bronisław Duch"

				attack_skill = 4
				defense_skill = 2

			}
		}

	}
}

# Offer Czechoslovakia Protection
country_event = {
	id = poland.209
	title = poland.209.t
	desc = poland.209.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_7tp_czechoslovakia
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #accept
		name = poland.209.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.8
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				POL = { has_war = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				GER = { 
					has_government = fascism
					is_in_faction_with = HUN
					is_in_faction_with = ROM
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				POL = { num_of_factories < 30 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CZE = { 
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
					is_in_faction = no
					has_war = no
					has_capitulated = no
				}
				POL = { 
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
					is_in_faction = no
					has_capitulated = no
				}
			}
			POL = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = CZE
					autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
					freedom_level = 0.95
				}
			}
			CZE = { 
				add_stability = -0.05
				add_ideas = POL_Liberty_Desire
			}
			POL = { country_event = poland.210 }
		}
	}

	option = { #decline
		name = poland.209.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				POL = { has_army_manpower = { size > 699999 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				POL = { has_army_manpower = { size > 899999 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				POL = { has_army_manpower = { size > 999999 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				POL = { has_army_manpower = { size > 1249999 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				POL = { num_of_factories > 50 }
			}
		}
		POL = { country_event = poland.211 }
	}
}

	title = news.1047.t
	desc = news.1047.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_polish_woronez
	
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {
		260 = { is_controlled_by = POL }
		260 = { is_owned_by = SOV }
		POL = { has_war_with = SOV }
        NOT = { has_global_flag = fall_of_woronez_pol }
	}
	
    immediate = {
		set_global_flag = fall_of_woronez_pol
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = {
		name = news.1047.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				TAG = POL
				TAG = SOV
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = news.1047.b
		trigger = { TAG = POL }
	}
	option = {
		name = news.1047.c
		trigger = { TAG = SOV }
	}
}

#rename city
country_event = {
	id = poland.961
	title = poland.961.t
	desc = poland.961.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_lithuanian_commonwealth

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = POL
		POL = {
			owns_state = 11	
            owns_state = 189
			owns_state = 879
		}
	}

	option = { #a great idea!
		name = poland.961.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		set_province_name = { id = 9438 name = "Poniewież"}
		set_province_name = { id = 6296 name = "Kowno Królewskie"}
		set_province_name = { id = 9483 name = "Szawle"}
		set_province_name = { id = 11312 name = "Mariampol"}
		set_province_name = { id = 6314 name = "Połąga"}
		set_province_name = { id = 3288 name = "Kłajpeda"}
		set_province_name = { id = 3320 name = "Wilno"}
		879 = { set_state_name = "Suwalszczyzna" }
		11 = { set_state_name = "Kowno Królewskie" }
		784 = { set_state_name = "Wilno" }
		991 = { set_state_name = "Litwa Górna" }
		189 = { set_state_name = "Zmudz" }
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.05
		set_global_flag = POL_cities_renamed
	}

	option = { #rather not
		name = poland.961.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		add_stability = -0.05 #because fuck you
	}

}

#rename general
country_event = {
	id = poland.965
	title = poland.965.t
	desc = poland.965.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_Rydz_Smigly_and_Stasys_Rasztikis

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = POL
		POL = {
            owns_state = 11
		}
	}

	option = { #a great idea!
		name = poland.965.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = 0.05
		set_global_flag = POL_rastykys_come
		create_corps_commander = {
	        name = "Stasys Raštikis"
	        picture = "Portrait_Lithuania_Stasys_Rastikis.dds"
	        traits = { career_officer cavalry_officer }
	        skill = 4
	        attack_skill = 2
	        defense_skill = 4
	        planning_skill = 2
	        logistics_skill = 2 
	    }
	}
	
	option = { #rather not
		name = poland.965.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_stability = -0.05 #because fuck you
	}

}

		202 = { is_owned_by = POL }

		226 = { is_owned_by = POL }
		198 = { is_owned_by = POL }
		193 = { is_owned_by = POL }
        NOT = { has_global_flag = Soviet_is_polish_pol }
	}
	
    immediate = {
		set_global_flag = Soviet_is_polish_pol
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}
	
	option = {
		name = news.972.a
		trigger = {
		    NOT = {
				TAG = POL
				TAG = SOV
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = news.972.b
		trigger = { TAG = POL }
	}
	option = {
		name = news.972.c
		trigger = { TAG = SOV }
	}
}

			base = 0
		}

#Demands for Serekunda
country_event = {
	id = poland.1010
	title = poland.1010.t
	desc = poland.1010.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_mansion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.1010.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = POL_smooth_talking_charmer }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				POL = { has_idea_with_trait = army_chief_offensive_prankster }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				701 = { is_controlled_by = ENG }
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					tag = ENG 
				}
				add_political_power = 150
			}
            POL = {
			    country_event = poland.1011
			    add_political_power = -20
			    set_province_name = { id = 4989 name = "Jakubów"}
			    transfer_state = 701
			    701 = { 
				    add_resource = {
					    type = rubber
					    amount = 9
					    state = 701
					}
					add_resource = {
						type = tungsten
						amount = 2
						state = 701
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
    option = { # rather not
		name = poland.1010.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

#Delete Generals
country_event = {
	id = poland.1069
	title = poland.1069.t
	desc = poland.1069.desc
	picture = GFX_POL_event_royal_castle
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
    fire_only_once = yes
	
    option = { #a great idea!
		name = poland.poland.1069.a
        ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		set_country_flag = Polish_Delete_Generals
		custom_effect_tooltip = remove_military_high_command
		remove_unit_leader = 3130 #Kazimierz Sosnkowski, general
		remove_unit_leader = 3137 #Franciszek_Kleeberg, general
		remove_unit_leader = 3138 #Wiktor_Thommee, general
	    remove_unit_leader = 3140 #Wilhelm_Orlik_Ruckemann, general
		remove_unit_leader = 3141 #Wladyslaw_Anders, general
		remove_unit_leader = 3142 #Michal_Tokarzewski_Karaszewicz, general 
		remove_unit_leader = 3139 #Stanisław_Grzmot_Skotnicki, general 
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = poland.1222
	title = news.1222.t
	desc = news.1222.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_polish_szczecin

	major = yes
	
	trigger = {
		9 = { is_controlled_by = POL }
		9 = { is_owned_by = CZE }
		POL = { has_war_with = CZE }
        NOT = { has_global_flag = fall_of_praque_pol }
	}
	
    immediate = {
		set_global_flag = fall_of_praque_pol
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	
	option = {
		name = news.1222.a
		trigger = { TAG = POL }
	}
}

# Event starting neutral civil war
country_event = {
	id = poland.1002
	title = poland.1002.t
	desc = poland.1002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_occupy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = neutrality_poland_civil_war
	}
	
	#civil war starts
	option = {
		name = poland.1002.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_capital = 86
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				ideology = fascism
				size = 0.5
				capital = 10
				states = { 10 92 88 762 91 89 996 997 97 933 90 95 96 94 93 863 984 784 864}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = POL
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_stability = 0.30
				set_war_support = 0.8
			}
			POL = { sound_effect = sp_pol_warsoviet }
			hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = poland.1016 hours = 6 } }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = poland.5220 hours = 6 } }
			hidden_effect = { 
				996 = {
					controller = {
						UKR = {
							declare_war_on = {
							target = PREV
							type = annex_everything
							}
						}
					}
				}				
			D01 = { country_event = poland.1069 }
			D02 = { country_event = poland.1069 }
			D04 = { country_event = poland.1069 }
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = POL_ARP_party_long name = POL_ARP_party }
			POL = { set_cosmetic_tag = POLK }
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_military_high_command
		    remove_unit_leader = 3128 #Rydz_Smigly_General, field marshal
		    remove_unit_leader = 3142 #Michal_Tokarzewski_Karaszewicz, general
		    remove_unit_leader = 3150 #Kazimierz_Fabrycy, general
			POL = {
            remove_ideas = POL_Rural_Unemployment
            add_ideas = POL_general_staff
		    }		
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.00
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.50
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.50
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.00
			}	
			set_stability = 0.9
			set_war_support = 0.8
		}
		set_stability = 0.30
		set_war_support = 0.8
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Władysław Sikorski"
			desc = "POLITICS_WLADYSLAW_SIKORSKI_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Poland_Wladyslaw_Sikorski.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = oligarchism
			traits = {
				POL_chief_staffer
			}
		}
		create_field_marshal = {
	           name = "Władysław Sikorski"
	           picture = "Portrait_Poland_Wladyslaw_Sikorski.dds"
	           traits = { war_hero offensive_doctrine fast_planner logistics_wizard cavalry_leader }
	           skill = 4
	           attack_skill = 4
	           defense_skill = 3
	           planning_skill = 3
	           logistics_skill = 3
		}
		create_corps_commander = {
	            name = "Wilhelm Orlik-Rückemann"
	            picture = "Wilhelm_Orlik_Ruckemann.dds"
	            traits = { career_officer armor_officer panzer_leader trait_engineer }
	            skill = 3
	            attack_skill = 2
	            defense_skill = 3
	            planning_skill = 3
	            logistics_skill = 3
		}
		create_corps_commander = {
	            name = "Wacław Stachiewicz"
	            picture = "Portrait_Poland_Waclaw_Stachiewicz.dds"
	            traits = { career_officer bearer_of_artillery }
	            skill = 2
	            attack_skill = 2
	            defense_skill = 2
	            planning_skill = 1
	            logistics_skill = 3
		}
		create_corps_commander = {
	            name = "Kazimierz Sosnkowski"
	            picture = "Kazimierz_Sosnkowski.dds"
	            traits = { career_officer infantry_leader cavalry_leader ranger trickster bearer_of_artillery   }
	            skill = 3
	            attack_skill = 4
          	    defense_skill = 4
         	    planning_skill = 3
	            logistics_skill = 3
		}
		create_corps_commander = {
	            name = "Franciszek Kleeberg"
	            picture = "Franciszek_Kleeberg.dds"
	            traits = { career_officer trickster swamp_fox trait_engineer commando }
	            skill = 3
	            attack_skill = 3
	            defense_skill = 4
	            planning_skill = 4
	            logistics_skill = 3
        }
        create_corps_commander = {
	            name = "Wiktor Thommée"
	            picture = "Wiktor_Thommee.dds"
	            traits = { career_officer skilled_staffer infantry_leader fortress_buster ambusher  }
	            skill = 3
	            attack_skill = 4
	            defense_skill = 4
	            planning_skill = 3
	            logistics_skill = 3
		}
		remove_unit_leader = 3146 #Franciszek_Wład, general 
		remove_unit_leader = 3145 #Władysław_Langner, general 
		remove_unit_leader = 3144 #Czesław_Młot_Fijałkowski, general

# Event starting neutral civil war
country_event = {
	id = poland.5222
	title = poland.5222.t
	desc = poland.5222.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_polish_occupy

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = neutrality_poland_civil_war
	}
	
	#civil war starts
	option = {
		name = poland.5222.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_capital = 86
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				ideology = fascism
				size = 0.5
				capital = 10
				states = { 10 92 88 762 91 89 996 997 97 933 90 863 95 96 94 93 864 784 865 98}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = POL
					has_government = fascism
				}
				set_stability = 0.30
				set_war_support = 0.8
			}
			POL = { sound_effect = sp_pol_warsoviet }
			hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = poland.1016 hours = 6 } }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = poland.5220 hours = 6 } }
			D01 = { country_event = poland.1069 }
			D02 = { country_event = poland.1069 }
			D04 = { country_event = poland.1069 }
			set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = POL_ARP_party_long name = POL_ARP_party }
			POL = { set_cosmetic_tag = POLK }
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_military_high_command
		    remove_unit_leader = 3128 #Rydz_Smigly_General, field marshal
		    remove_unit_leader = 3142 #Michal_Tokarzewski_Karaszewicz, general
		    remove_unit_leader = 3150 #Kazimierz_Fabrycy, general
			POL = {
            remove_ideas = POL_Rural_Unemployment
            add_ideas = POL_general_staff
		    }		
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.00
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.50
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.50
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.00
			}

			name = "Władysław Sikorski"
			desc = "POLITICS_WLADYSLAW_SIKORSKI_DESC"

	           skill = 4
	           attack_skill = 4
	           defense_skill = 3
	           planning_skill = 3
	           logistics_skill = 3
		}
		create_corps_commander = {
	            name = "Wilhelm Orlik-Rückemann"
	            picture = "Wilhelm_Orlik_Ruckemann.dds"
	            traits = { career_officer armor_officer panzer_leader trait_engineer }
